DROP TABLE FUEL CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE FUEL(
    Fuel_num  NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->    index
    Fuel_type VARCHAR(12) NOT NULL, -->  
    CONSTRAINT FUEL_PK PRIMARY KEY (Fuel_num),
    CONSTRAINT FUEL_TYPE_UK UNIQUE (Fuel_type)
);
  
DROP TABLE COLOR CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE COLOR(
    Color_num   NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->  index
    Color_name  VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, -->  
    CONSTRAINT COLOR_PK PRIMARY KEY (Color_num),
    CONSTRAINT COLOR_NAME_UK UNIQUE(Color_name)
);

DROP TABLE TRANSMISSION CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;  
CREATE TABLE TRANSMISSION(
    Transmission_num    NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    Transmission_type   VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT TRANSMISSION_PK PRIMARY KEY (Transmission_num),
    CONSTRAINT TRANSMISSION_TYPE_UK UNIQUE (Transmission_type)
);

DROP TABLE CONDITION CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;  
CREATE TABLE CONDITION(
    Condition_num   NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    Grade           VARCHAR(15)  NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT CONDITION_PK PRIMARY KEY (Condition_num),
    CONSTRAINT CONDITION_GRADE_UK UNIQUE (Grade)
);

DROP TABLE ENGINE_DISPLACEMENT CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE ENGINE_DISPLACEMENT(
    ED_num    NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    ED_value   NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT ENGINE_DISPLACEMENT_PK PRIMARY KEY (ED_num),
    CONSTRAINT ENGINE_DISPLACEMENT_UK UNIQUE (ED_value)
);

DROP TABLE CATEGORY CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE CATEGORY(
    Category_num    NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    Category_name   VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT CATEGORY_PK PRIMARY KEY (Category_num),
    CONSTRAINT CATEGORY_NAME_UK UNIQUE (Category_name)
);

DROP TABLE MAKE CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE MAKE(
    Make_num  NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->  index
    Make_name VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, -->  
    Nation    VARCHAR(8) NOT NULL,  --> Domestic or Import   
    CONSTRAINT MAKE_PK PRIMARY KEY (Make_num),
    CONSTRAINT MAKE_NAME_UK UNIQUE (Make_name)
);

DROP TABLE MODEL CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE MODEL(
    Model_num    NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->  index
    Model_name   VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, -->  
    Manufacturer NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->   foreign key(FK) MODEL -> MAKE
    CONSTRAINT MODEL_PK PRIMARY KEY (Model_num),
    CONSTRAINT MODEL_NAME_UK UNIQUE (Model_name),
    CONSTRAINT MODEL_MANUFACTURER_FK FOREIGN KEY (Manufacturer) REFERENCES MAKE(Make_num)
);

DROP TABLE DETAILED_MODEL CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE DETAILED_MODEL
  (
    Detail_num          NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->   index
    Detail_Name         VARCHAR(45) NOT NULL, -->   
    Parent_model        NUMBER,           -->   foreign key
    CONSTRAINT DETAILED_MODEL_PK PRIMARY KEY (Detail_num),
    CONSTRAINT DETAILED_MODEL_PARENT_MODEL_FK FOREIGN KEY (Parent_model) REFERENCES MODEL(Model_num)
  );

DROP TABLE ACCOUNT CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE ACCOUNT
  (
    Account_num NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->  
    Birth_date  DATE,                 -->  
    Id          VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL, -->  id
    Pw          VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, -->  pw
    Phone       VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, -->  
    Email       VARCHAR(50),          -->  email
    Sex         CHAR,                 -->   M or F
    Job         VARCHAR(50),          -->  
    User_type   VARCHAR(8) NOT NULL,  -->   customer or seller => maximum length 8
    Fname       VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, -->  
    Lname       VARCHAR(15) NOT NULL, -->  
    Zipcode     VARCHAR(5),           -->  5  
    Addr       VARCHAR(120),          -->   
    CONSTRAINT ACCOUNT_PK PRIMARY KEY(Account_num),
    CONSTRAINT ACCOUNT_ID_UK UNIQUE(Id)
    -->CONSTRAINT ACCOUNT_BIRTHDATE_CK CHECK(Birth_date <= current_date)
  );

DROP TABLE VEHICLE CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE VEHICLE
  (
    Reg_num           NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->    
    Transmission      NUMBER NOT NULL, -->   => '', '', ''
    Release_date      DATE NOT NULL,        --> 
    Vin               VARCHAR(6) NOT NULL, -->   
    Condition         NUMBER NOT NULL,                 
    Is_sold           VARCHAR(5) default 'FALSE' NOT NULL,                 
    Displacement      NUMBER NOT NULL,
    Price             NUMBER NOT NULL,      -->    
    Detailed_model    NUMBER NOT NULL,  --> 
    Registerer        NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->     ()  foregin key
    Category          NUMBER NOT NULL,
    Is_hybrid         VARCHAR(5) default 'FALSE' NOT NULL,
    Mpg               NUMBER NOT NULL,
    Mileage           NUMBER NOT NULL, -->            
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_PK PRIMARY KEY (Reg_num),
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_VIN_UK UNIQUE(Vin),
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_TRANSMISSION_FK FOREIGN KEY (Transmission) REFERENCES TRANSMISSION(Transmission_num),
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_CONDITION_FK FOREIGN KEY (CONDITION) REFERENCES CONDITION(Condition_num),
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_DISPLACEMENT_FK FOREIGN KEY (Displacement) REFERENCES ENGINE_DISPLACEMENT(ED_num),
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_DETAILED_MODEL_FK FOREIGN KEY (Detailed_model) REFERENCES Detailed_model(Detail_num),
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_REGISTERER_FK FOREIGN KEY (Registerer) REFERENCES ACCOUNT(Account_num),
    CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_CATEGORY_FK FOREIGN KEY (Category) REFERENCES CATEGORY(Category_num)
  );

DROP TABLE INSURANCE_RECORD CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE INSURANCE_RECORD
  (
    Accident_vehicle NUMBER NOT NULL, -->         foreign key
    Date_time        DATE NOT NULL,       -->   =>      partial key
    Cost             NUMBER(5) NOT NULL,  -->  
    CONSTRAINT INSURANCE_RECORD_ACCIDENT_FK FOREIGN KEY (Accident_vehicle) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num),
    CONSTRAINT INSURANCE_RECORD_PK PRIMARY KEY (Accident_vehicle, Date_time)
  );

DROP TABLE "ORDER" CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE "ORDER"
  (
    Order_num      NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->   index
    Order_Date     DATE NOT NULL,        --> 
    Buyer          NUMBER NOT NULL , -->       foregin key
    Seller         NUMBER NOT NULL , -->       foregin key
    Reg_num        NUMBER NOT NULL,  -->        foreign key
    CONSTRAINT ORDER_PK PRIMARY KEY (Order_num),
    CONSTRAINT ORDER_BUYER_FK FOREIGN KEY (Buyer) REFERENCES ACCOUNT(Account_num),
    CONSTRAINT ORDER_SELLER_FK FOREIGN KEY (Seller) REFERENCES ACCOUNT(Account_num),
    CONSTRAINT ORDER_REG_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Reg_num) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num)
  );
DROP TABLE USES CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE USES
  (
    Reg_num    NUMBER NOT NULL, --> 
    Fuel_num   NUMBER NOT NULL, -->     foregin key
    CONSTRAINT USES_FUEL_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Fuel_num) REFERENCES FUEL(Fuel_num),
    CONSTRAINT USES_REG_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Reg_num) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num),
    CONSTRAINT USES_PK PRIMARY KEY (Fuel_num, Reg_num)
  );
DROP TABLE PAINTS CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
CREATE TABLE PAINTS(
    Reg_num     NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    Color_num   NUMBER  NOT NULL,
    CONSTRAINT PAINTS_REG_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Reg_num) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num),
    CONSTRAINT PAINTS_COLOR_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Color_num) REFERENCES COLOR(Color_num),
    CONSTRAINT PAINTS_PK PRIMARY KEY (Reg_num, Color_num)
);

CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER Order_Made
AFTER INSERT ON "ORDER"
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN 
UPDATE vehicle
SET Is_sold='TRUE'
WHERE Reg_num=:new.Reg_num;
END;
/
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER Order_Cancel
AFTER DELETE ON "ORDER"
FOR EACH ROW
BEGIN 
UPDATE vehicle
SET Is_sold='FALSE'
WHERE Reg_num=:old.Reg_num;
END;
/

-->Added DDL
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER VEHICLE_Inserted
AFTER INSERT ON VEHICLE
FOR EACH ROW
DECLARE 
Fuel_count Number(1);
BEGIN 
SELECT COUNT(*) 
INTO Fuel_count
FROM USES
WHERE reg_num=:new.reg_num;
If (Fuel_count>=2) Then
UPDATE vehicle
SET Is_hybrid='TRUE' 
where reg_num=:new.reg_num;
End if;
END;
/

alter table vehicle
add Is_viewable VARCHAR2(5) default 'TRUE' NOT NULL;
commit;

--  ? ?? stored procedure 
CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE buyingProcess(
regNum IN VEHICLE.REG_NUM%TYPE,
buyerNum IN ACCOUNT.ACCOUNT_NUM%TYPE)
IS 
orderNum "ORDER".ORDER_NUM%TYPE;
sellerNum VEHICLE.REGISTERER%TYPE;
BEGIN
SELECT Max(ORDER_NUM)+1
INTO orderNum
FROM "ORDER";

SELECT REGISTERER
INTO sellerNum
FROM VEHICLE
WHERE REG_NUM=regNum;

INSERT INTO "ORDER" VALUES(orderNum,TO_DATE(sysdate,'yy/mm/dd'),buyerNum,sellerNum,regNum);
UPDATE VEHICLE
SET Is_Sold='TRUE'
WHERE REG_NUM=regNum;
END;
/
commit;
-- vehicle viewable option ?
alter table vehicle
add Is_viewable VARCHAR2(5) default 'TRUE' NOT NULL;
commit;


-- ORDER attribute ?? nullable?? ??
ALTER TABLE "ORDER"
MODIFY
(
    "BUYER" NUMBER NULL,
    "SELLER" NUMBER NULL,
    "REG_NUM" NUMBER NULL
);
-- VEHICLE attribute ?? nullable?? ??
ALTER TABLE VEHICLE
MODIFY
(
    "REGISTERER" NUMBER NULL
);

-- ORDER table? Buyer? ????, Account? ?? ???  NULL? ?? ? ? ? ??.
ALTER TABLE "ORDER"
DROP CONSTRAINT ORDER_BUYER_FK;
ALTER TABLE "ORDER"
ADD CONSTRAINT ORDER_BUYER_FK FOREIGN KEY (Buyer) REFERENCES ACCOUNT(Account_num) ON DELETE SET NULL;

-- ORDER table? Seller? ????, Account? ?? ???  NULL? ?? ? ? ? ??.
ALTER TABLE "ORDER"
DROP CONSTRAINT ORDER_SELLER_FK;
ALTER TABLE "ORDER"
ADD CONSTRAINT ORDER_SELLER_FK FOREIGN KEY (Seller) REFERENCES ACCOUNT(Account_num) ON DELETE SET NULL;

-- ORDER table? reg_num? ????, Vehicle? ?? ???  NULL? ?? ? ? ? ??.
ALTER TABLE "ORDER"
DROP CONSTRAINT ORDER_REG_NUM_FK;
ALTER TABLE "ORDER"
ADD CONSTRAINT ORDER_REG_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Reg_num) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num) ON DELETE SET NULL;

-- INSURANCE TABLE ? , VEHICLE? ?? ?? INSURANCE RECORD? ??? ? ??? ??.
ALTER TABLE INSURANCE_RECORD
DROP CONSTRAINT INSURANCE_RECORD_ACCIDENT_FK;
ALTER TABLE "INSURANCE_RECORD"
ADD CONSTRAINT INSURANCE_RECORD_ACCIDENT_FK FOREIGN KEY (Accident_vehicle) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num) ON DELETE CASCADE;

--VEHICLE? Registerer? ????, ACCOUNT? ?? ??? ?,  NULL? ?? ?? ??.
ALTER TABLE VEHICLE
DROP CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_REGISTERER_FK;
ALTER TABLE VEHICLE
ADD CONSTRAINT VEHICLE_REGISTERER_FK FOREIGN KEY (Registerer) REFERENCES ACCOUNT(Account_num) ON DELETE SET NULL;

-- USES table? , VEHICLE? ????, ?? ? ??? ?? ?? ?????.
ALTER TABLE USES
DROP CONSTRAINT USES_REG_NUM_FK;
ALTER TABLE USES
ADD CONSTRAINT USES_REG_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Reg_num) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num) ON DELETE CASCADE;

-- PAINTS table? , VEHICLE? ????, ?? ? ??? ?? ?? ?????.
ALTER TABLE PAINTS
DROP CONSTRAINT PAINTS_REG_NUM_FK;
ALTER TABLE PAINTS
ADD CONSTRAINT PAINTS_REG_NUM_FK FOREIGN KEY (Reg_num) REFERENCES VEHICLE(Reg_num) ON DELETE CASCADE;
